The REST Admin API is a legacy API as of October 1, 2024. Starting April 1, 2025, all new public apps must be built exclusively with the [GraphQL Admin API](/docs/api/admin-graphql). For details and migration steps, visit our [migration guide](/docs/apps/build/graphql/migrate).

2026-01latest

# Product Image

Ask assistant

Requires `products` access scope.

**Requires `products` access scope.:**

Important

Listing, creating, updating, and deleting product images is deprecated as of REST API 2025-01. For more information, refer to the [guide to the new product model](/docs/api/admin/migrate/new-product-model).

**Important:** 


Listing, creating, updating, and deleting product images is deprecated as of REST API 2025-01. For more information, refer to the [guide to the new product model](/docs/api/admin/migrate/new-product-model).

Products are easier to sell if customers can see pictures of them, which is why there are **product images**.

![](/assets/api/reference/product-image.png)

Any product may have up to 250 images, and images can be in .png, .gif or .jpg format.

**Best practices for naming image files**

To successfully upload or update images, follow these best practices when naming your image files:

* Don't use spaces in the file name. Example: `my file name.png`
* Don't begin your file name with symbols, like "!". Example: `!my_file_name.png`
* Avoid using periods before the file extension. Example: `my_file_name..png`
* Avoid long, complicated file names that contain excess characters.

  Example: `my_---_file_---_name_---.png`

  /admin/api/latest/products/{product\_id}/images.json](/docs/api/admin-rest/latest/resources/product-image#post-products-product-id-images)

## The Product Image resource

[Anchor to](/docs/api/admin-rest/latest/resources/product-image#resource-object-properties) 

### Properties

---

created\_at

->[![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-CQ7q9aDJ.svg)![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-dark-CtivyDg_.svg)

createdAt](/docs/api/admin-graphql/latest/objects/MediaImage#field-MediaImage.fields.createdAt)

The date and time when the product image was created. The API returns this value in [ISO 8601 format](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601).

---

id

integer**integer**

int64**int64**

->[![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-CQ7q9aDJ.svg)![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-dark-CtivyDg_.svg)

id](/docs/api/admin-graphql/latest/objects/MediaImage#field-MediaImage.fields.id)

A unique numeric identifier for the product image.

---

position

The order of the product image in the list. The first product image is at position 1 and is the "main" image for the product.

---

product\_id

deprecated**deprecated**

The id of the product associated with the image.

---

variant\_ids

deprecated**deprecated**

An array of variant ids associated with the image.

---

src

->[![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-CQ7q9aDJ.svg)![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-dark-CtivyDg_.svg)

url](/docs/api/admin-graphql/latest/objects/Image#field-Image.fields.url)

Specifies the location of the product image. This parameter supports [Liquid filters](/api/liquid/filters/image_url) that you can use to retrieve modified copies of the image.

---

width

->[![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-CQ7q9aDJ.svg)![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-dark-CtivyDg_.svg)

width](/docs/api/admin-graphql/latest/objects/Image#field-Image.fields.width)

Width dimension of the image which is determined on upload.

---

height

->[![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-CQ7q9aDJ.svg)![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-dark-CtivyDg_.svg)

height](/docs/api/admin-graphql/latest/objects/Image#field-Image.fields.height)

Height dimension of the image which is determined on upload.

---

updated\_at

->[![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-CQ7q9aDJ.svg)![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-dark-CtivyDg_.svg)

updatedAt](/docs/api/admin-graphql/latest/objects/MediaImage#field-MediaImage.fields.updatedAt)

The date and time when the product image was last modified. The API returns this value in [ISO 8601 format](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601).

---

  #### response

  ```liquid
  HTTP/1.1 200 OK{"image":{"id":1001473917,"alt":null,"position":1,"product_id":632910392,"created_at":"2026-01-09T19:36:49-05:00","updated_at":"2026-01-09T19:36:49-05:00","admin_graphql_api_id":"gid://shopify/MediaImage/1072273210","width":110,"height":140,"src":"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0005/4838/0009/files/rails_logo.gif?v=1768005409","variant_ids":[]}}
  ```
* #### Create a new product image using a source URL that will be downloaded by Shopify

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  curl -d '{"image":{"src":"http://example.com/rails_logo.gif"}}' \
  -X POST "https://your-development-store.myshopify.com/admin/api/2026-01/products/632910392/images.json" \
  -H "X-Shopify-Access-Token: {access_token}" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  const { admin, session } = await authenticate.admin(request);

  const image = new admin.rest.resources.Image({session: session});

  image.product_id = 632910392;
  image.src = "http://example.com/rails_logo.gif";
  await image.save({
    update: true,
  });
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  # Session is activated via Authentication
  test_session = ShopifyAPI::Context.active_session

  image = ShopifyAPI::Image.new(session: test_session)
  image.product_id = 632910392
  image.src = "http://example.com/rails_logo.gif"
  image.save!
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  // Session is built by the OAuth process

  const image = new shopify.rest.Image({session: session});
  image.product_id = 632910392;
  image.src = "http://example.com/rails_logo.gif";
  await image.save({
    update: true,
  });
  ```

  #### response

  ```liquid
  HTTP/1.1 200 OK{"image":{"id":1001473919,"alt":null,"position":4,"product_id":632910392,"created_at":"2026-01-09T19:37:01-05:00","updated_at":"2026-01-09T19:37:01-05:00","admin_graphql_api_id":"gid://shopify/MediaImage/1072273212","width":110,"height":140,"src":"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0005/4838/0009/files/rails_logo20260109-27647-dpv8dd.gif?v=1768005421","variant_ids":[]}}
  ```

## [Anchor to GET request, Receive a list of all Product Images](/docs/api/admin-rest/latest/resources/product-image#get-products-product-id-images) get Receive a list of all Product Images

[![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-CQ7q9aDJ.svg)![](https://cdn.shopify.com/shopifycloud/shopify-dev/production/assets/assets/images/logos/GraphQL-dark-CtivyDg_.svg)

product](/docs/api/admin-graphql/latest/queries/product)

Get all product images

### [Anchor to Parameters of Receive a list of all Product Images](/docs/api/admin-rest/latest/resources/product-image#get-products-product-id-images-parameters)Parameters

---

api\_version

string**string**

required**required**

---

product\_id

string**string**

required**required**

---

fields

comma-separated list of fields to include in the response

---

since\_id

Restrict results to after the specified ID

---

### examples

* #### Get all product images for a product

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  curl -X GET "https://your-development-store.myshopify.com/admin/api/2026-01/products/632910392/images.json" \
  -H "X-Shopify-Access-Token: {access_token}"
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  await admin.rest.resources.Image.all({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
  });
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  # Session is activated via Authentication
  test_session = ShopifyAPI::Context.active_session

  ShopifyAPI::Image.all(
    session: test_session,
    product_id: 632910392,
  )
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  // Session is built by the OAuth process

  await shopify.rest.Image.all({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
  });
  ```

  #### response

  ```liquid
  HTTP/1.1 200 OK{"images":[{"id":850703190,"alt":null,"position":1,"product_id":632910392,"created_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","updated_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","admin_graphql_api_id":"gid://shopify/MediaImage/498048120","width":123,"height":456,"src":"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0005/4838/0009/products/ipod-nano.png?v=1767996251","variant_ids":[]},{"id":562641783,"alt":null,"position":2,"product_id":632910392,"created_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","updated_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","admin_graphql_api_id":"gid://shopify/MediaImage/1071517486","width":123,"height":456,"src":"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0005/4838/0009/products/ipod-nano-2.png?v=1767996251","variant_ids":[808950810]},{"id":378407906,"alt":null,"position":3,"product_id":632910392,"created_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","updated_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","admin_graphql_api_id":"gid://shopify/MediaImage/220090436","width":123,"height":456,"src":"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0005/4838/0009/products/ipod-nano.png?v=1767996251","variant_ids":[]}]}
  ```
* #### Get all product images for a product after a specified ID

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  curl -X GET "https://your-development-store.myshopify.com/admin/api/2026-01/products/632910392/images.json?since_id=850703190" \
  -H "X-Shopify-Access-Token: {access_token}"
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  await admin.rest.resources.Image.all({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
    since_id: "850703190",
  });
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  # Session is activated via Authentication
  test_session = ShopifyAPI::Context.active_session

  ShopifyAPI::Image.all(
    session: test_session,
    product_id: 632910392,
    since_id: "850703190",
  )
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  // Session is built by the OAuth process

  await shopify.rest.Image.all({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
    since_id: "850703190",
  });
  ```

  #### response

  ```liquid
  HTTP/1.1 200 OK{"images":[{"id":1001473915,"alt":null,"position":4,"product_id":632910392,"created_at":"2026-01-09T19:36:32-05:00","updated_at":"2026-01-09T19:36:32-05:00","admin_graphql_api_id":"gid://shopify/MediaImage/1072273208","width":110,"height":140,"src":"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0005/4838/0009/files/rails_logo.gif?v=1768005392","variant_ids":[]}]}
  ```

### examples

* #### Show product image

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  curl -X GET "https://your-development-store.myshopify.com/admin/api/2026-01/products/632910392/images/850703190.json" \
  -H "X-Shopify-Access-Token: {access_token}"
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  await admin.rest.resources.Image.find({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
    id: 850703190,
  });
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  # Session is activated via Authentication
  test_session = ShopifyAPI::Context.active_session

  ShopifyAPI::Image.find(
    session: test_session,
    product_id: 632910392,
    id: 850703190,
  )
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  // Session is built by the OAuth process

  await shopify.rest.Image.find({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
    id: 850703190,
  });
  ```

  #### response


### examples

* #### Get a count all product images

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  curl -X GET "https://your-development-store.myshopify.com/admin/api/2026-01/products/632910392/images/count.json" \
  -H "X-Shopify-Access-Token: {access_token}"
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  await admin.rest.resources.Image.count({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
  });
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  # Session is activated via Authentication
  test_session = ShopifyAPI::Context.active_session

  ShopifyAPI::Image.count(
    session: test_session,
    product_id: 632910392,
  )
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  // Session is built by the OAuth process

  await shopify.rest.Image.count({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
  });
  ```

  #### response

  ```liquid
  HTTP/1.1 200 OK{"count":3}
  ```
* #### Get a count of all product images after a specified ID

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  curl -X GET "https://your-development-store.myshopify.com/admin/api/2026-01/products/632910392/images/count.json?since_id=850703190" \
  -H "X-Shopify-Access-Token: {access_token}"
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  await admin.rest.resources.Image.count({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
    since_id: "850703190",
  });
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  # Session is activated via Authentication
  test_session = ShopifyAPI::Context.active_session

  ShopifyAPI::Image.count(
    session: test_session,
    product_id: 632910392,
    since_id: "850703190",
  )
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  // Session is built by the OAuth process

  await shopify.rest.Image.count({
    session: session,
    product_id: 632910392,
    since_id: "850703190",
  });
  ```

  #### response

  ```liquid
  HTTP/1.1 200 OK{"count":0}
  ```

### examples

* #### Modify an image and change its position and alt tag content

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  curl -d '{"image":{"id":850703190,"position":2,"alt":"new alt tag content"}}' \
  -X PUT "https://your-development-store.myshopify.com/admin/api/2026-01/products/632910392/images/850703190.json" \
  -H "X-Shopify-Access-Token: {access_token}" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  const { admin, session } = await authenticate.admin(request);

  const image = new admin.rest.resources.Image({session: session});

  image.product_id = 632910392;
  image.id = 850703190;
  image.position = 2;
  image.alt = "new alt tag content";
  await image.save({
    update: true,
  });
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  # Session is activated via Authentication
  test_session = ShopifyAPI::Context.active_session

  image = ShopifyAPI::Image.new(session: test_session)
  image.product_id = 632910392
  image.id = 850703190
  image.position = 2
  image.alt = "new alt tag content"
  image.save!
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  // Session is built by the OAuth process

  const image = new shopify.rest.Image({session: session});
  image.product_id = 632910392;
  image.id = 850703190;
  image.position = 2;
  image.alt = "new alt tag content";
  await image.save({
    update: true,
  });
  ```

  #### response

  ```liquid
  HTTP/1.1 200 OK{"image":{"id":850703190,"alt":"new alt tag content","position":1,"product_id":632910392,"created_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","updated_at":"2026-01-09T19:36:34-05:00","admin_graphql_api_id":"gid://shopify/MediaImage/498048120","width":123,"height":456,"src":"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0005/4838/0009/products/ipod-nano.png?v=1767996251","variant_ids":[]}}
  ```
* #### Modify an image; add a metafield

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  curl -d '{"image":{"id":850703190,"metafields":[{"key":"my_new_metafield","value":"my_new_value","type":"single_line_text_field","namespace":"tags"}]}}' \
  -X PUT "https://your-development-store.myshopify.com/admin/api/2026-01/products/632910392/images/850703190.json" \
  -H "X-Shopify-Access-Token: {access_token}" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  const { admin, session } = await authenticate.admin(request);

  const image = new admin.rest.resources.Image({session: session});

  image.product_id = 632910392;
  image.id = 850703190;
  image.metafields = [
    {
      "key": "my_new_metafield",
      "value": "my_new_value",
      "type": "single_line_text_field",
      "namespace": "tags"
    }
  ];
  await image.save({
    update: true,
  });
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  # Session is activated via Authentication
  test_session = ShopifyAPI::Context.active_session

  image = ShopifyAPI::Image.new(session: test_session)
  image.product_id = 632910392
  image.id = 850703190
  image.metafields = [
    {
      "key" => "my_new_metafield",
      "value" => "my_new_value",
      "type" => "single_line_text_field",
      "namespace" => "tags"
    }
  ]
  image.save!
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  // Session is built by the OAuth process

  const image = new shopify.rest.Image({session: session});
  image.product_id = 632910392;
  image.id = 850703190;
  image.metafields = [
    {
      "key": "my_new_metafield",
      "value": "my_new_value",
      "type": "single_line_text_field",
      "namespace": "tags"
    }
  ];
  await image.save({
    update: true,
  });
  ```

  #### response

  ```liquid
  HTTP/1.1 200 OK{"image":{"id":850703190,"alt":null,"position":1,"product_id":632910392,"created_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","updated_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","admin_graphql_api_id":"gid://shopify/MediaImage/498048120","width":123,"height":456,"src":"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0005/4838/0009/products/ipod-nano.png?v=1767996251","variant_ids":[]}}
  ```
* #### Modify an image; add it to product variants

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  curl -d '{"image":{"id":850703190,"variant_ids":[808950810,457924702]}}' \
  -X PUT "https://your-development-store.myshopify.com/admin/api/2026-01/products/632910392/images/850703190.json" \
  -H "X-Shopify-Access-Token: {access_token}" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json"
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  const { admin, session } = await authenticate.admin(request);

  const image = new admin.rest.resources.Image({session: session});

  image.product_id = 632910392;
  image.id = 850703190;
  image.variant_ids = [
    808950810,
    457924702
  ];
  await image.save({
    update: true,
  });
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  # Session is activated via Authentication
  test_session = ShopifyAPI::Context.active_session

  image = ShopifyAPI::Image.new(session: test_session)
  image.product_id = 632910392
  image.id = 850703190
  image.variant_ids = [
    808950810,
    457924702
  ]
  image.save!
  ```

  ##### 

  ```liquid
  // Session is built by the OAuth process

  const image = new shopify.rest.Image({session: session});
  image.product_id = 632910392;
  image.id = 850703190;
  image.variant_ids = [
    808950810,
    457924702
  ];
  await image.save({
    update: true,
  });
  ```

  #### response

  ```liquid
  HTTP/1.1 200 OK{"image":{"id":850703190,"alt":null,"position":1,"product_id":632910392,"created_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","updated_at":"2026-01-09T17:04:11-05:00","admin_graphql_api_id":"gid://shopify/MediaImage/498048120","width":123,"height":456,"src":"https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/0005/4838/0009/products/ipod-nano.png?v=1767996251","variant_ids":[808950810,457924702]}}
  ```
